* takes care of producing the return type information automatically.\\n41:  *\\n42:  * <p>A DeserializationSchema must be {@link Serializable} because its instances are often part of\\n43:  * an Serializable, ResultTypeQueryable<T> {\\n49:     /**\\n50:      * Initialization method for the schema.
